    <script>
     (function(){
            var translates = {
                ru: {
                    title: 'Выберите язык сайта по-умолчанию',
                    button: 'Подтвердить'
                },
                en: {
                    title: 'Select a default site language',
                    button: 'Confirm'
                },
                jp: {
                    title: 'デフォルトのサイト言語を選択してください',
                    button: '確認する'
                },
                cn: {
                    title: '选择默认的网站语言',
                    button: '确认'
                },
                la: {
                    title: 'Seleccione un idioma predeterminado del sitio',
                    button: 'Confirme'
                },
                br: {
                    title: 'Selecione um idioma padrão do site',
                    button: 'Confirme'
                },
            };
            var $toggle          = $('#language_toggle'),
                $dropdown        = $('#language_options'),
                $language_title  = $('#language_title'),
                $language_button = $('#language_button')

            $('#language_options input').click(function(event){
                var $input = $(this);

                $toggle.html($input.parent().text());
                $toggle.prepend($input.next('img').clone());
                $toggle.removeClass('active js_autohide');
                $dropdown.addClass('hidden');
                $language_title.text(translates[this.value].title);
                $language_button.text(translates[this.value].button);
            });
            $toggle.click(function(event){
                event.preventDefault();

                if ($toggle.hasClass('active')) {
                    $toggle.removeClass('active js_autohide');
                    $dropdown.addClass('hidden');
                } else {
                    $toggle.addClass('active js_autohide');
                    $dropdown.removeClass('hidden');
                }
            });
        })();
    </script>

   <script>
    // app.ready(function(){
    $(function(){
      var swiper,
      remoteUrl   = '/ajax-banners', // url for ajax request
          isTouchable = 'ontouchstart' in document.documentElement;

      function onSlideChange(s, callback) {
        callback();

        if (remoteUrl && s.activeIndex !== 1) {
          s.lockSwipes();

          $.get(remoteUrl, function(html){
            remoteUrl = null;

            if (s.params.autoplay) s.stopAutoplay();
            if (s.params.loop) s.destroyLoop();

            $('.banner-placeholder', s.wrapper).remove();
            s.wrapper.append(html);

            if (s.params.loop) s.createLoop();

            s.update();
            s.unlockSwipes();
            s.slideTo(s.activeIndex, 0);

            if (s.params.autoplay) s.startAutoplay();

            callback();
          });
        }
      }

      swiper = new Swiper('#banner', {
        autoplay: 10000,  // autoplay delay
        loop: true,
        nextButton: isTouchable ? null : '#banner .swiper-button-next',
        pagination: '#banner .swiper-pagination',
        paginationClickable: true,
        prevButton: isTouchable ? null : '#banner .swiper-button-prev',
        slidesPerView: 1,
        spaceBetween: 0,
        onInit: function(s) {
          if ($(s.slides[s.activeIndex]).hasClass('dark')) {
            s.paginationContainer.addClass('swiper-pagination-white');
          } else {
            s.paginationContainer.removeClass('swiper-pagination-white');
          }
        },
        onSlideChangeEnd: function(s) {
          onSlideChange(s, function(){
            if ($(s.slides[s.activeIndex]).hasClass('dark')) {
              s.paginationContainer.addClass('swiper-pagination-white');
            } else {
              s.paginationContainer.removeClass('swiper-pagination-white');
            }
          });
        }
      });
    });
    // });
   </script>

   <script>
    $(window).load(function(){ // run script after page loaded
			var swiper,
				width       = $(window).width(),
				isTouchable = 'ontouchstart' in document.documentElement;

			if (!isTouchable) {
				$('#enterprise').append(
					'<div class="swiper-button-next"></div> ' +
					'<div class="swiper-button-prev"></div>'
				);
			}

			$('#enterprise .js_swiper_anchor').click(function(event){
				event.preventDefault();
				window.location.href = this.href;
			});
			swiper = new Swiper('#enterprise', {
				centeredSlides: false,
				initialSlide: 0,
				loop: true,
				threshold: 10,
				nextButton: isTouchable ? null : '#enterprise .swiper-button-next',
				pagination: '#enterprise .swiper-pagination',
				paginationClickable: true,
				prevButton: isTouchable ? null : '#enterprise .swiper-button-prev',
				slidesPerView: Math.min($('#enterprise .swiper-slide').length, 4),
				spaceBetween: 0,
				breakpoints: {
					1232: {
						centeredSlides: false,
						slidesPerView: 'auto',
						initialSlide: 0,
					},
					767: {
						centeredSlides: true,
						slidesPerView:'auto',
						initialSlide: 1
					}
				},
				onAfterResize: function(s){
					var breakpoint  = s.getActiveBreakpoint(),
						screenWidth = $(window).width();

					if (screenWidth !== width) {
						width = screenWidth;

						if (breakpoint === '767') {
							s.slideTo(1, 0);
						} else {
							s.slideTo(0, 0);
						}

						if (breakpoint !== 'max') {
							s.slides.prop('style', null); // fix to remove width
						}

						if (s.slides.not('.swiper-slide-duplicate').length <= s.params.slidesPerView) {
							s.paginationContainer.hide();
							s.disableTouchControl();
						} else {
							s.paginationContainer.show();
							s.enableTouchControl();
						}
					}
				},
				onInit: function(s) {
					if (s.slides.not('.swiper-slide-duplicate').length <= s.params.slidesPerView) {
						s.paginationContainer.hide();
						s.disableTouchControl();
					}
				}
			});
		});
   </script>

   <script>
    (function () {
            var swiper,
                isTouchable = 'ontouchstart' in document.documentElement,
                width = $(window).width();

            // if (!isTouchable) {
            //   $('#industry_participants').append(
            //     '<div class="swiper-button-next"></div> ' +
            //     '<div class="swiper-button-prev"></div>'
            //   );
            // }

            swiper = new Swiper('#industry_participants', {
                autoplay: 0, // autoplay delay
                loop: true,
                // nextButton: isTouchable ? null : '#industry_participants .swiper-button-next',
                pagination: '#industry_participants .swiper-pagination',
                paginationClickable: true,
                // prevButton: isTouchable ? null : '#industry_participants .swiper-button-prev',
                slidesPerView: 5,
                slidesPerGroup: 5,
                spaceBetween: 0,
                breakpoints: {
                    767: {
                        slidesPerView: 2,
                        slidesPerGroup: 2
                    }
                },
                onAfterResize: function (s) {
                    var screenWidth = $(window).width();

                    if (screenWidth !== width) {
                        width = screenWidth;

                        if (s.slides.length <= s.params.slidesPerView) {
                            s.paginationContainer.hide();
                            s.disableTouchControl();
                        } else {
                            s.paginationContainer.show();
                            s.enableTouchControl();
                        }
                    }
                },
                onInit: function (s) {
                    if (s.slides.not('.swiper-slide-duplicate').length <= s.params.slidesPerView) {
                        s.paginationContainer.hide();
                        s.disableTouchControl();
                    }
                }
            });
        })();
   </script>

   <div class="footer-subscribe">
    <div class="w container">
     <h5 class="join-us">
      <a href="/career">
       Join us! We are hiring!
      </a>
     </h5>
     <form action="/server/server.php?action=subscribe" class="footer-subscribe-form" id="footer_subscribe">
      <input name="lang" type="hidden" value="en"/>
      <label>
       Join 30,000+ readers of our Zabbix News
      </label>
      <div class="oneinput">
       <input autocomplete="off" name="email" placeholder="Enter your email" type="text"/>
       <button class="subscribe_newsletter" type="submit">
       </button>
      </div>
     </form>
     <script>
      $('#footer_subscribe').submit(function(event){
					event.preventDefault();

					var field = this.email,
						value = field.value;

					if (app.helpers.isValidEmail(field.value)) {
                        fetch($(this).attr('action'), {
                            method: 'POST',
                            body: new FormData(this)
                        });

						// on success
						this.reset();

						var $msg = $('<span class="success">Your message sent!</span>')
							.insertBefore(this.email)
							.click(function(event){
								event.preventDefault();

								$msg.removeClass('show');
							});

						setTimeout(function(){
							$msg.addClass('show');
						}, 0);

						setTimeout(function(){
							$msg.removeClass('show');
						}, 5000);

						setTimeout(function(){
							$(field).blur();
						}, 600);
					} else {
						// on error
						$(field)
							.addClass('invalid')
							.off('keyup')
							.on('keyup', function(){
								if (value.length !== this.value.length) {
									$(this)
										.removeClass('invalid')
										.prev()
										.remove();
								}
							})
							.before('<span class="error">Please enter valid email address</span>');
					}
				});
     </script>
